<text>Reckless Brewery foremerly known as Wet n' Reckless, which got burned down due to fire accident.

Beer Choices: Plenty , ~ 30 taps
*** Top 5 Beers (No-Particular Order) ***
Badger Don’t Care : Dark n Crisp
Spicy Boy : IPA with spice
Merlout : Stout
Upside Brown: Nutty Brown Ale
Super Destroyer  Malty
***Ambiance***
Location is wisely thought, right next to Ballast point. I came here due to parking issues at Ballast Point. I looked parking on opposite complex and ended up going there.
Indoor, is very tight not many seating areas.
No Outdoor seating

***Prices***
Little on the expensive side for what they offer.
Taster size = 4 oz. $1.50-$3, $15 for a set of 6 I paid
Half pour size $3:50
Full size pour: $6

***Food***
Not at this place. Food truck, sometimes.

***Try this***
variety of board games
foosball room
free popcorn
video games

***Highs***
Nothing other than you get high

***Lows***
Too tiny place
Not too many IPA choices
No Food

<review>This is easily one of my favorite stops after a long day at work.  The place is very casual and comfortable and the customers are always friendly and interesting.  Each time I have been in there's been new beers to try, but also certain core selections are always up.

You can't go wrong with a pour of Honey Badger, Dude Abides rye, or Down and Out stout, but there are also cool specialties like the mead, Hell's Belge (dark belgian), and Super Ridiculous stout.  There's also a sake and merlot beer available sometimes!

The bartenders are very attentive and will let you try a splash of any beer that interests you before committing to a pint or taster flight.  Then its time to strike up some fun conversations or just relax and people watch.<//review>< Date>
1453133314662< /Date>

<resp>None<//resp>< text>
It's a small place, located across the street from Ballast Point in an office building.

Their beers are on the stronger side, and I liked their fruitier beers, like the Precious Endeavor (?...Can't recall the name).
Merlout was an interesting one. A stout with strong hints of wine.

I like my IPAs very very hoppy. The ones here are not hoppy. So be warned if that's what you look for.

Free Popcorn! A variety of seasoning salts and sauces are available to spice it up as well.

Does not make my top 5 in San Diego, but I'm glad I came. :)<//text>

< text>
Love these guys!   We use them every year during the Monte Fireworks show for an amazing evening on the water with a beautiful, front row view of the fireworks.  They have a small mini bar and offer a limited selection of wine and beer.  They also have hot chocolate for the kids and serve cookies as a snack.   Great for the whole family.   Bring something warm to wear and a blanket as it can get cold being out on the open water.  Also, crew and staff are great (bring some cash to tip these guys - they work hard to give you a memorable experience).</text>

< Review>
My husband and I took the 1.5 hour sail.  First time for us and we had a blast.  The boat is big and rides smooth.  There were a lot of people but plenty of room for everyone.  We saw a whale and some sea otters.  The staff were all super friendly, very professional, and extremely courteous.  We go to Santa Cruz every summer and this will now be a tradition for us.   The price is very reasonable.  One thing to note...a lot of the reviews mention meters at the dock.  There were very few meters and they were all taken.  We paid $12.50 to park in the Harbor Lot.  So be prepared just in case.  Thanks O'Neil Yacht Charters for a blast on the sea!< /Review>

< review>
What great customer service!  We missed our cruise.  We were scheduled to go on Thursday night during the big beach party held at Santa Cruz Beach. My husband dropped me off where we were supposed to board, and then he went to find a parking space.  After driving around for over 30 minutes, he still could not find a space.  The sweet girl that was handing out boarding passes waited for us as long as she possibly could, and offered to give us cruising credit for another date.  However, we were leaving town early the next morning.  Shortly after leaving,  she called to tell us that she had spoken with the Captain, and we would be receiving a full refund.  Thank you both for going above and beyond!  We will definitely be cruising with you guys the next time we are in Santa Cruz!< /review>

I buy most of my vaping juices and accessories online because the four previous brick & mortar shops I've gone into, the staff were indifferent, smug, and/or downright douchebags, and I'm not in the habit of paying money to be condescended to.

I only went to So Cal Vape Lounge because I had a stressful morning and was in desperate need of some e-juice. So Cal was close by and I didn't want to wait 2 days for an online order.

Really quite nice.  I've been to the Thursday evening services a few times now, and each visit has been a very relaxed and no-pressure experience, which is right up my alley.  I'm fairly new to meditation, and this place is where I've had the most 'success'.  The atmosphere is very conducive, and the lectures/sermons have been very accessible and pleasantly lacking in that old secretive woo-woo.  As a person with a lifetime of not-great experiences regarding faith and God/religion, this place and the teachings of Yoganada are a very welcome and positive experience.< /Text>

< Text>
I had always imagined that there must be someplace like this out there somewhere, maybe in India or Thailand, but certainly not in the US. The first “sermon” I heard was like light from heaven filling my soul. I spent a year attending SRF and reading Paramahansa Yogananda’s teachings and I gained much from the experience, but that first visit to SRF Center, hearing my first guru speak, was one of the spiritual experiences I will remember for the rest of my life. Realizing there were other people who thought similar to me in spiritual matters, instead of it being a hypothetical, blew me away. I no longer live in California, but I will always fondly remember my time at SRF!<//Text>

<Resp>None< /Resp>< Review>
So we are back to extreme restrictions. You know what that means.  Only places with patio and outside seating can be open.
Which also means you are in luck with Rib Joint.  They have an outside patio and a fire pit.   I've seen Neda get that pit started and it is impressive.
But back to the real reason to go to Rib Joint, the food!!!!
Sam is still working the grill and get getting your BBQ favorites prepared.
My favorite is to stop in and order my food and then enjoy a cocktail or cold beer, depending on my mood while I wait.
My wife's favorite is always the burger and onion rings, but we really love the hand made chicken tenders as well.  Or the brisket.... or the ribs.....  Well actually we haven't had a single item on the menu that we wouldn't order again!!!< /Review>

< Review>
Ive been wanting to try this place for some time. Stopped in a few months ago to place a pick up order. This is a family owned business and found everyone there to be warm and inviting. Since it was my first time here i ordered a large portion of beef ribs, large portion of pork ribs, whole chicken, several appetizers, all sides offered and their chicken soup. The bbq items were great, the corn bread was moist and delicious, they make a terrific homemade chicken soup that my wife and i enjoyed...even the ranch dressing is homemade and you can tell the difference. <review>As you walk in to this establishment, it's like stepping back in time when 'Mom n Pop' operated restaurants are at every corner. < text>
We were looking forward to a good rib dinner during our stay at Doheny State Beach. After our visit to the Rib Joint...I wish we would have just stayed at our campground and barbequed our own! When we arrived at the typical dinner hour the place was empty...This should have been our 1st clue not to eat there. The only folks there looked like they were regulars at the bar. By the looks of them and by the foul language coming from their mouths that should have been our 2nd clue not to eat there. When the ribs arrived they were very dry and overcooked. They gave us a side of barbecue sauce but even that wasn't any good. When I took the leftovers home to my husband he said they were the worst ribs he had ever eaten. It's too bad because the location was good, the waitress was very nice, but the food just wasn't good. I was warned by someone to go elsewhere and I wish I would have taken their advice. I feel bad being so critical because it looked like a family owned business and I wish I could support them. They need to work on their cooking and it just might be a good place to eat if they did.< /text>

5</rating>
< Review>
Huddart Park is a beautiful park for hike around multiple trails. It is thickly wooded and the trails are well marked.

One can choose trails which are flat or have moderate elevation. There is open space where one can play simple games. There is a sand volley ball court too. And a badminton court. Lots of picnic areas around.

Ample parking across multiple parking lots. Entry fee is $6 per car. Make sure that you carry exact cash if possible, as if the booth is not manned you'll have to drop the fee in a box.

Overall, a fantastic place to spend time with friends and family.</Review>

<user>113515181944940915487</user><text>Lonely Trail to Richards Road loop trail is part of Huddart park. Park hours are till 5 pm so parking outside would be a good option, in case you can not get back by 5pm. Park has a big parking lot. Restrooms are available at the trailhead. It’s around an 8.5 mile moderate hike. We completed it in 4hrs. Trail is shaded, lots of Redwood trees. Keep the trail map handy all the time as there are many diversions, and easy to get off track. There are logs and fallen trees across the trail, be careful while crossing them. Overall nice, quiet hike, good workout. Bonus- enjoy melodious bird chirping while hiking :)< /text>< GmapID>

I loved hiking in this park with my boyfriend on Christmas Eve. The trails are nice and fairly easy to understand where you’re going to next. Don’t let the $6 (cash only) entrance fee detract from enjoying this awesome place. There is tons of parking, great picnic and bbq areas with grass, picnic tables, pavilions, etc. There are sand volleyball courts and playgrounds.

We just completed the Crystal Springs via Dean Trail loop and got to enjoy the whole place to ourselves.

Oh and it’s a great baby friendly hike area because you are under a lot of tree cover most of the time without too much exposure.</text>

< text>
Nice park with extensive picnic and camping facilities.   It also has a network of trails in towering redwoods which are cool in the summer and beautiful after winter rains.   Even when the picnic grounds are crowded, a hiker can find solitude on the trails.   The park also houses a bow and arrow golf course run by  Kings Mountain Archery  and a section of the Bay Ridge Trail along Skyline Blvd.    However, the park does charge $6 for parking thereby losing one star.</text>

Ranger recommended a 5 mile loop (Crystal spring to Dean trail), which is largely shared and passes through lush redwood groves. Huddart County Park offers many trails for day hikers and trail runners. Situated right next to Phleger Estate (Part of the Golden Gate National Recreation Area) enables hikers to enjoy longer hikes by going up through Huddart and coming back down through Phleger Estate. Huddart offers picnic areas and restrooms as well as free parking to seniors!</Text>

<text>What a beautiful park! First ... logistics: $6 entry fee, no animals. If you qualify for those, this is a place you must visit. The trails are really well upkept and the picnic areas are numerous and diverse. You can picnic on a blanket in the grass or avoid any crowds and relax under the trees at one of the other picnic areas (you could even come here for a weekend hiking date). There is a ton of tree cover here so it's a great place to come on a hot day for either a picnic or moderate difficulty hike. (Translated by Google) Fully-equipped park, special parking spaces, parking fee 6 yuan, self-pay.
Many trails are very easy or need physical strength, and can even cross to other parks. It is usually closed at 5pm on weekends and it is 6am on weekends, be careful of being locked!
There is a large group venue for large parties.
This is a logging site a hundred years ago, so there are many historical traces, and the big tree roots that were cut down are a pity.

里面有很大的团体活动场所，适合较大的party。
